       <div style="border-bottom: 1px solid #bebebe;margin-bottom:15px;">
        <h1>
         Trusted Personal Injury Attorney in Los Angeles, CA
        </h1>
        <p>
         If you or someone you know has been hurt in an accident in California, its time to hire a trusted personal injury attorney in Los Angeles from Madison Law Group. At our Los Angeles personal injury law firm, our attorneys have years of experience representing individuals who need help getting the compensation that they deserve as a result of their accident. We provide in-depth legal knowledge to personal injury cases and also have experience defending against insurance companies, individuals, or businesses.
         <a href="https://www.dmv.org/insurance/statute-of-limitations-and-personal-injury.php">
          California statute of limitations
         </a>
         requires that a personal injury lawsuit is brought forth to the court within two years from the date of your injury. This makes it increasingly important to hire a California personal injury attorney as soon as possible after you have sustained injuries.
        </p>
        <h2>
         Are You Looking for a Personal Injury Lawyer in the Greater Los Angeles Area?
        </h2>
        <p>
         Having a California
         <a href="https://www.madisonlawgroup.com/about-madison-law-group/">
          personal injury lawyer
         </a>
         by your side increases your chances of winning your case. Our team of personal injury attorneys in Los Angeles not only have extensive experience to handle your case, but also have the resources needed to represent you with ease. They work diligently to protect the rights of their clients 24/7. Also, when it comes to hiring a personal injury attorney, they have the experience needed to properly assess your situation to decide what the right course of action is. Whether filing an insurance claim, taking it to court, negotiating a settlement, or going to trial, our team of Southern California personal injury attorneys in Beverly Hills, Westwood, West Los Angeles, Santa Monica, and all of the surrounding Los Angeles communities can help give you peace of mind when you need it most. Best of all, we can offer objective insight into your particular legal situation and help you make the right decisions for your future.
        </p>
        <h3>
         Have You Been Hurt in a Car Accident?
        </h3>
        <p>
         If you or a loved one have been injured in a
         <a href="https://www.madisonlawgroup.com/practice-areas/legal-consideration-car-accident/">
          car accident
         </a>
         in or around Los Angeles, California then you know the costs of the damages as a result of your accident. Our team of car accident attorneys can help you to recover the compensation that you deserve as a result of your injuries. Whether a truck, car, or a pedestrian accident, our legal team always has your back. We will investigate the cause of your accident, to determine who is negligent and gather all evidence needed to make your case as strong as possible. No matter what type of injury you have sustained, our job is to get you the money you deserve as a result of your injuries. Some things you can be compensated for include permanent loss of income or lost wages until you can work again, medical bills, pain and suffering, emotional distress, or wrongful death. At Madison Law Group, we will take the proper time needed to listen to your case and decide whether or not you have a viable personal injury case.
        </p>
        <h3>
         Are You Looking for an Experienced Motorcycle Accident Attorney?
        </h3>
        <p>
         If you or a loved one has been involved in a
         <a href="https://www.madisonlawgroup.com/practice-areas/motorcycle-accident-attorney-2/">
          motorcycle accident
         </a>
         in or around Santa Monica, then you need the skills and experience of a California lawyer from Madison Law Group to represent you. With a proven track record of success helping motorcycle accidents victims, we work hard to recover the maximum compensation for our clients who may have suffered from head, back, brain, or spinal cord injuries. These serious injuries can lead to a lifetime of medical bills and rehabilitation expenses, and in severe cases, the inability to work any longer. Our team of lawyers can investigate your accident and determine what caused your accident and who was negligent. We understand all of the insurance laws associated with motorcycles in the State of California as well. All motorcycle drivers must have insurance that includes liability insurance coverage, which covers bodily injury suffered by others in a crash and property damage. There are minimum liability limits that must be followed, and we can determine if the driver carried them. If not, we have to call your insurance carrier to fill the gap in the compensation you deserve.
        </p>
        <h3>
         Contact Madison Law Group if You Have Been Injured in an Accident
        </h3>
        <p>
         Our team of Los Angeles personal injury attorneys understands how important it is for victims and families of personal injury cases to have highly-rated legal representation by their side. When you want to hear about our legal experience and what we can offer you regarding legal services, call our California law office at 310-201-7676 or 1-866-LEGAL-911. We represent personal injury clients in Los Angeles, Beverly Hills, Westwood, Santa Monica, and all of the surrounding Los Angeles communities. We cant wait to hear from you today.
        </p>
       </div>
       <h2>
        There are five major factors you should know and consider when hiring a law firm:
       </h2>
       <p>
        <span class="questFirst">
         1. Who You Are Hiring To Represent You.
        </span>
       </p>
       <p>
        If you choose to hire Madison Law Group, your handling attorney will be Kyle K. Madison, Esq. The truth is, it is not the law firm that you hire, but the attorney that handles your case that is important. Many law firms advertise that they have experienced attorneys and have compensated millions of dollars for their clients. But when you retain their firm, a junior associate ends up working on your case that may not have the experience of those attorney advertised or promised. The founder of Madison Law Group is attorney Kyle K. Madison who has been in practice for 12 years representing solely thousands of injured Plaintiffs like you. Prior to becoming an attorney, Mr. Madison was a licensed insurance agent working closely on handling insurance matters, which provided him with in-depth knowledge and experience of the defense side of each case from an insurance companies strategies and perspectives. This experience has earned Mr. Madison a great reputation in the industry and has helped him have an impressively high success rate in settling cases with insurance companies prior to lengthy litigation.
       </p>
       <p>
        2. Your Experience and Trust With Your Attorney.
       </p>
       <p>
        The experience you have with the attorney you hire is key. When you are dealing with an injury, the last thing you want to worry about is your legal needs not being handled properly. If its a serious injury, you may not be able to work or do daily activities as you were able to do prior to the accident. This may bring about great frustration in your life and you will not want to worry about your legal rights in addition to coming back to health. Your attorney must have not only extensive experience to handle your case, but he or she must be trustworthy. Someone you can rely on to inform you about your legal rights, someone who can inform you about the right direction to proceed at each step of your case, and most importantly, someone to return your calls. The experience you will have as Kyle Madisons client is bar none because you can put your legal worries aside knowing that you are in great hands while you recover from your personal injury. Mr. Madison has personally trained his staff to handle your file professionally and efficiently. They are courteous, responsive and experienced. All personnel at Madison Law Group adhere to a strict 24 hour call back policy so that you will never be kept in the dark about your case and your experience will be pleasant under difficult circumstances.
       </p>
       <p>
        3. The Right Guidance In Determining The Value Of Your Case.
       </p>
       <p>
        Each personal injury case is evaluated on the type of injury that you have, medical bills accrued in the end of your treatment or bills that may be accrued in the future that a doctor recommends, amount of pain and suffering you had to endure, loss of past and future earnings, and the severity of property damage. If you have not been through a personal injury case before, you will need guidance as to how to record and receive such benefits available to you. For example, if you do not have health insurance and cannot afford medical care when you have been injured, Madison Law Group will provide you with names of qualified and experienced medical professionals who will work on your case on a lien basis. This means that they will provide care for you and hold off on monetary compensation until your case is finished. In another example, if you have been involved in a car accident and your car is totaled or not drivable, you may need a rental car or a referral to a body shop. Madison Law Group will guide you through it by recommending certified auto bodies in your area and taking care of your rental needs while your car is being repaired or you are compensated if its a total loss. Without such guidance, you may lose the maximum value your case is worth.
       </p>
       <p>
        4. Maximum Results.
       </p>
       <p>
        Be cautious if an attorney tells you what your case is worth without a proper evaluation, which requires time and in depth information about your injuries, loss of earnings, your pain and suffering and liability. To properly evaluate a case and bring forth maximum results takes time, effort and experience. Depending on your injury and your circumstances, certain experts such as surgeons, economists, neuropsychologists, pain management specialists, life care planners, and liability experts, need to be retained to prove your case at trial. Many times, hiring such experts well in advance helps maximize the value of your case prior to trial because readiness for trial is single most important factor for a successful settlement. If necessary, we hire the right expert to prove your case well in advance of trial. As a result, your case is prepared and will be ripe to receive maximum monetary recovery.
       </p>
       <p>
        5. Compensation To Madison Law Group.
       </p>
       <p>
        You do not have to pay anything out of your pocket to retain Madison Law Group. Our law firm works on a contingency fee basis, which mean we dont recover any fees unless we win your case and recover money for you. Only in that instance, we will take a percentage of your recovery (generally one third).
       </p>
       <p>
        Madison Law Group will provide you with the services outlined above. This is why we are The Firm You Can Trust.
       </p>

   <script type="text/javascript">
    var recaptchaWidgets = [];
 var recaptchaCallback = function() {
 	var forms = document.getElementsByTagName( 'form' );
 	var pattern = /(^|\s)g-recaptcha(\s|$)/;
 
 	for ( var i = 0; i < forms.length; i++ ) {
 		var divs = forms[ i ].getElementsByTagName( 'div' );
 
 		for ( var j = 0; j < divs.length; j++ ) {
 			var sitekey = divs[ j ].getAttribute( 'data-sitekey' );
 
 			if ( divs[ j ].className && divs[ j ].className.match( pattern ) && sitekey ) {
 				var params = {
 					'sitekey': sitekey,
 					'type': divs[ j ].getAttribute( 'data-type' ),
 					'size': divs[ j ].getAttribute( 'data-size' ),
 					'theme': divs[ j ].getAttribute( 'data-theme' ),
 					'badge': divs[ j ].getAttribute( 'data-badge' ),
 					'tabindex': divs[ j ].getAttribute( 'data-tabindex' )
 				};
 
 				var callback = divs[ j ].getAttribute( 'data-callback' );
 
 				if ( callback && 'function' == typeof window[ callback ] ) {
 					params[ 'callback' ] = window[ callback ];
 				}
 
 				var expired_callback = divs[ j ].getAttribute( 'data-expired-callback' );
 
 				if ( expired_callback && 'function' == typeof window[ expired_callback ] ) {
 					params[ 'expired-callback' ] = window[ expired_callback ];
 				}
 
 				var widget_id = grecaptcha.render( divs[ j ], params );
 				recaptchaWidgets.push( widget_id );
 				break;
 			}
 		}
 	}
 };
 
 document.addEventListener( 'wpcf7submit', function( event ) {
 	switch ( event.detail.status ) {
 		case 'spam':
 		case 'mail_sent':
 		case 'mail_failed':
 			for ( var i = 0; i < recaptchaWidgets.length; i++ ) {
 				grecaptcha.reset( recaptchaWidgets[ i ] );
 			}
 	}
 }, false );
   </script>
   <!-- BEGIN recaptcha, injected by plugin wp-recaptcha-integration  -->
   <script type="text/javascript">
    function get_form_submits(el){
 					var form,current=el,ui,type,slice = Array.prototype.slice,self=this;
 					this.submits=[];
 					this.form=false;
 
 					this.setEnabled=function(e){
 						for ( var s=0;s<self.submits.length;s++ ) {
 							if (e) self.submits[s].removeAttribute('disabled');
 							else  self.submits[s].setAttribute('disabled','disabled');
 						}
 						return this;
 					};
 					while ( current && current.nodeName != 'BODY' && current.nodeName != 'FORM' ) {
 						current = current.parentNode;
 					}
 					if ( !current || current.nodeName != 'FORM' )
 						return false;
 					this.form=current;
 					ui=slice.call(this.form.getElementsByTagName('input')).concat(slice.call(this.form.getElementsByTagName('button')));
 					for (var i = 0; i < ui.length; i++) if ( (type=ui[i].getAttribute('TYPE')) && type=='submit' ) this.submits.push(ui[i]);
 					return this;
 				}
   </script>
